Name                                            := Rock Colony Module
Description                                     := Materials needed to start a colony on a rock planet.
Picture Number                                  := 1
Maximum Level                                   := 2
Tonnage Space Taken Formula                     := 400 / [%Level%]
Tonnage Structure Formula                       := 400 / [%Level%]
Cost Minerals Formula                           := 6000 / [%Level%]
Cost Organics Formula                           := 6000 / [%Level%]
Cost Radioactives Formula                       := 2000 / [%Level%]

Ordnance Amount Used Formula                    := 0
Can Be Placed On Vehicle Types                  := Ship
Can Be Placed In Ship Sections                  := Inner Hull, Outer Hull
Component Type List                             := Technological
General Group                                   := Colonization
Custom Group                                    := 0
Number Of Requirements                          := 2
Requirements Evaluation Availability            := AND
Requirements Evaluation Allows Placement        := TRUE
Requirements Evaluation Allows Usage            := TRUE
Requirement 1 Description                       := Empire must have at least tech level 1 in Rock Planet Colonization.
Requirement 1 Formula                           := Get_Empire_Tech_Level("Rock Planet Colonization") >= 1
Requirement 2 Description                       := Empire must have a rock homeworld to get the advanced module.
Requirement 2 Formula                           := iif([%Level%] >= 2, Empire_Has_Home_Planet_Type("Rock"), TRUE)
Number Of Abilities                             := 2
Ability 1 Type                                  := Planet Colonize Type 1

Requirement 2 Formula                           := Get_Design_Ability_Component_Count("Master Computer") <= 1
